// Partially Observable bar-tailed_godwit_b Example

(variables
	(pop  s1 s2 s3 s4)
	(node3 	low 	med 	high)
	(node4 	low 	med 	high)
	(node5 	low 	med 	high)
	(node2 	low 	med 	high)
	(model  rise0cm rise100cm rise200cm)
)

// Obs prob of each breeding state is perfect= 1.
(observations	(pobs o1 o2 o3 o4)
				(obs3 	lo_ 	mid 	hi_)
				(obs4 	lo_ 	mid 	hi_)
				(obs5 	lo_ 	mid 	hi_)
				(obs2 	lo_ 	mid 	hi_)
)

//initial belief
init [*	(pop   (s1 (0.0))(s2 (0.0))(s3 (0.0))(s4 (1.0)))
		(node3 	(low	(1.0)) 	(med	(0)) 	(high	(0)))
		(node4 	(low	(1.0)) 	(med	(0)) 	(high	(0)))
		(node5 	(low	(1.0)) 	(med	(0)) 	(high	(0)))
		(node2 	(low	(1.0)) 	(med	(0)) 	(high	(0)))
		(model	(rise0cm	(0.33)) (rise100cm	(0.33)) (rise200cm	(0.33)))
]

//unnormalized declaration
unnormalised

//decision diagrams

//no action at node x
dd noaction3
(node3	(low		(node3'			(low(1))		(med(0))		(high(0))))
		(med	(node3'			(low(0.075))		(med(0.925))		(high(0))))
		(high	(node3'			(low(0))		(med(0.075))		(high(0.925))))
)
enddd

dd noaction4
(node4	(low		(node4'			(low(1))		(med(0))		(high(0))))
		(med	(node4'			(low(0.075))		(med(0.925))		(high(0))))
		(high	(node4'			(low(0))		(med(0.075))		(high(0.925))))

enddd

//action at node x

//model transitions
dd modeldd
(model	(rise0cm		(model'	(rise0cm(0.95))	(rise100cm(0.05))	(rise200cm(0))))
		(rise100cm		(model'	(rise0cm(0))	(rise100cm(0.95))	(rise200cm(0.05))))
		(rise200cm		(model'	(rise0cm(0))	(rise100cm(0))	(rise200cm(1))))
)
enddd

//observation function
dd popOF
(pobs'	(o1	(pop'	(s1	(1.0))	(s2	(0.0))	(s3	(0.0))	(s4	(0.0))))
		(o2	(pop'	(s1	(0.0))	(s2	(1.0))	(s3	(0.0))	(s4	(0.0))))
		(o3	(pop'	(s1	(0.0))	(s2	(0.0))	(s3	(1.0))	(s4	(0.0))))
		(o4	(pop'	(s1	(0.0))	(s2	(0.0))	(s3	(0.0))	(s4	(1.0))))
)
enddd
